       </div>This page provides an overview of the various discussions and requests taking place throughout English Wikipedia. To <b>ask a question</b> or <b>make a request</b>, see the <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Request_directory" title="Wikipedia:Request directory">request directory</a></b> to locate the appropriate venue(s). For a listing of current collaborations, tasks, and news, see the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Community_portal" title="Wikipedia:Community portal">Community portal</a>.

          <th style="text-align:left; font-size:115%; padding:1em; font-weight:normal; background:#BDD8FF;"><b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Backlog" title="Wikipedia:Backlog">Cleanup requests</a></b> </th>

          <td> <p>Articles transcluding a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Template_messages/Cleanup" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Template messages/Cleanup">cleanup template</a>. </p><p>Click any linked number for that category's articles prioritized by their number of incoming links. </p>

          <td> 
           <div role="navigation" class="navbox" aria-labelledby="Note_to_editors:Please_search_for_existing_articles_on_any_request._If_an_article_exists,_but_not_at_the_requested_title,_please_create_a_redirect.Be_sure_requests_meet_Wikipedia&amp;#039;s_inclusion_criteria._Fulfilled_requests_need_to_be_removed_manually." style="padding:3px">

               <td class="navbox-abovebelow" colspan="2">
                <div id="Note_to_editors:Please_search_for_existing_articles_on_any_request._If_an_article_exists,_but_not_at_the_requested_title,_please_create_a_redirect.Be_sure_requests_meet_Wikipedia&amp;#039;s_inclusion_criteria._Fulfilled_requests_need_to_be_removed_manually.">
                 <b>Note to editors:</b>
                 <br>Please <b><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Search&amp;fulltext=Search&amp;ns0=1&amp;redirs=1">search</a></span></b> for existing articles on any request. If an article exists, but not at the requested title, please <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:How_to_make_a_redirect" title="Wikipedia:How to make a redirect">create a redirect</a></b>.
                 <br>Be sure requests meet Wikipedia's <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Notability" title="Wikipedia:Notability">inclusion criteria</a></b>. Fulfilled requests need to be removed manually.
                </div></td>
